boots
============

Artifact Name: Pair of Leather Boots of Fëanor
Type = boots
Symbol = No symbol defined
Color = No color defined
Flags = []
Values = ['SPEED[15]', 'RES_NEXUS[1]']
Item Description = 
This wondrous pair of leather boots once sped Fëanor, creator of the 
Silmarils and the mightiest of the Eldar, to fulfill his hero's challenge 
and do battle for a Middle-Earth held in thrall.  "Dear-bought those songs 
shall be accounted, and yet shall be well-bought.  For the price could be 
no other."

Type = boots
Symbol = No symbol defined
Color = No color defined

Item Description = 
And they hewed off Gelmir's hands and feet, and his head last, within
sight of the Elves, and left him. By ill chance there stood Gwindor
of Nargothrond, the brother of Gelmir. Now his wrath was kindled to
madness, and he leapt forth on horseback, and many riders with him;
and they pursued the heralds and slew them, and drove on deep into
the main host.
